CREATE TABLE face_recognition (face_id INT PRIMARY KEY, user_id INT REFERENCES users(user_id), face_data BYTEA, timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ)</t><s>SHOW TABLES;</s>

CREATE TABLE users (user_id INT PRIMARY KEY, full_name VARCHAR(50), age INT, gender VARCHAR(10), height DECIMAL(5,2), weight DECIMAL(5,2))</t><s>show indexes from iris_scans;</s>
